11// SX1272 specific register map
12#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_REF 0x43
13#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_1 0x44
14#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_2 0x45
15#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_3 0x46
16#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_PLL_HOP 0x4B
17#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_TCXO 0x58
18#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_PA_DAC 0x5A
19#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_PLL 0x5C
20#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_PLL_LOW_PN 0x5E
21#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_FORMER_TEMP 0x6C
22#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_BIT_RATE_FRAC 0x70
23
24// SX1272 LoRa modem settings
25// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_FRF_MSB + REG_FRF_MID + REG_FRF_LSB
26#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FRF_MSB 0xE4 // 7 0 carrier frequency setting: f_RF = (F(XOSC) * FRF)/2^19
27#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FRF_MID 0xC0 // 7 0 where F(XOSC) = 32 MHz
28#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FRF_LSB 0x00 // 7 0 FRF = 3 byte value of FRF registers
29
30// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_MODEM_CONFIG_1
31#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_BW_125_00_KHZ 0b00000000 // 7 6 bandwidth: 125 kHz
32#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_BW_250_00_KHZ 0b01000000 // 7 6 250 kHz
33#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_BW_500_00_KHZ 0b10000000 // 7 6 500 kHz
34#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CR_4_4 0b00000000 // 5 3 error coding rate: 4/4 (undocumented)
35#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CR_4_5 0b00001000 // 5 3 4/5
36#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CR_4_6 0b00010000 // 5 3 4/6
37#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CR_4_7 0b00011000 // 5 3 4/7
38#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CR_4_8 0b00100000 // 5 3 4/8
39#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_HEADER_EXPL_MODE 0b00000000 // 2 2 explicit header mode
40#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_HEADER_IMPL_MODE 0b00000100 // 2 2 implicit header mode
41#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_RX_CRC_MODE_OFF 0b00000000 // 1 1 CRC disabled
42#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_RX_CRC_MODE_ON 0b00000010 // 1 1 CRC enabled
43#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_LOW_DATA_RATE_OPT_OFF 0b00000000 // 0 0 low data rate optimization disabled
44#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_LOW_DATA_RATE_OPT_ON 0b00000001 // 0 0 low data rate optimization enabled, mandatory for SF 11 and 12 with BW 125 kHz
45
46// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_MODEM_CONFIG_2
47#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_AUTO_OFF 0b00000000 // 2 2 LNA gain set by REG_LNA
48#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_AUTO_ON 0b00000100 // 2 2 LNA gain set by internal AGC loop
49
50// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_VERSION
51#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_CHIP_VERSION 0x22
52
53// SX1272 FSK modem settings
54// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_OP_MODE
55#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_NO_SHAPING 0b00000000 // 4 3 data shaping: no shaping (default)
56#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FSK_GAUSSIAN_1_0 0b00001000 // 4 3 FSK modulation Gaussian filter, BT = 1.0
57#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FSK_GAUSSIAN_0_5 0b00010000 // 4 3 FSK modulation Gaussian filter, BT = 0.5
58#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FSK_GAUSSIAN_0_3 0b00011000 // 4 3 FSK modulation Gaussian filter, BT = 0.3
59#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_OOK_FILTER_BR 0b00001000 // 4 3 OOK modulation filter, f_cutoff = BR
60#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_OOK_FILTER_2BR 0b00010000 // 4 3 OOK modulation filter, f_cutoff = 2*BR
61
62// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_PA_RAMP
63#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_LOW_PN_TX_PLL_OFF 0b00010000 // 4 4 use standard PLL in transmit mode (default)
64#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_LOW_PN_TX_PLL_ON 0b00000000 // 4 4 use lower phase noise PLL in transmit mode
65
66// RADIOLIB_SX127X_REG_SYNC_CONFIG
67#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FIFO_FILL_CONDITION_SYNC_ADDRESS 0b00000000 // 3 3 FIFO will be filled when sync address interrupt occurs (default)
68#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_FIFO_FILL_CONDITION_ALWAYS 0b00001000 // 3 3 FIFO will be filled as long as this bit is set
69
70// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_REF
71#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_REFERENCE_LEVEL 0x13 // 5 0 floor reference for AGC thresholds: AgcRef = -174 + 10*log(2*RxBw) + 8 + AGC_REFERENCE_LEVEL [dBm]
72
73// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_1
74#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_STEP_1 0x0E // 4 0 1st AGC threshold
75
76// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_2
77#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_STEP_2 0x50 // 7 4 2nd AGC threshold
78#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_STEP_3 0x0B // 4 0 3rd AGC threshold
79
80// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_AGC_THRESH_3
81#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_STEP_4 0xD0 // 7 4 4th AGC threshold
82#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_AGC_STEP_5 0x0B // 4 0 5th AGC threshold
83
84// RADIOLIB_SX1272_REG_PLL_LOW_PN
85#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_PLL_LOW_PN_BANDWIDTH_75_KHZ 0b00000000 // 7 6 low phase noise PLL bandwidth: 75 kHz
86#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_PLL_LOW_PN_BANDWIDTH_150_KHZ 0b01000000 // 7 6 150 kHz
87#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_PLL_LOW_PN_BANDWIDTH_225_KHZ 0b10000000 // 7 6 225 kHz
88#define RADIOLIB_SX1272_PLL_LOW_PN_BANDWIDTH_300_KHZ 0b11000000 // 7 6 300 kHz (default)
89
90/*!
91 \class SX1272
92 \brief Derived class for %SX1272 modules. Also used as base class for SX1273.
93 Both modules use the same basic hardware and only differ in parameter ranges.
94*/
95class SX1272: public SX127x {
96 public:
97
98 // constructor
99
100 /*!
101 \brief Default constructor. Called from Arduino sketch when creating new LoRa instance.
102 \param mod Instance of Module that will be used to communicate with the %LoRa chip.
103 */
104 SX1272(Module* mod); // cppcheck-suppress noExplicitConstructor
105
106 // basic methods
107
108 /*!
109 \brief %LoRa modem initialization method. Must be called at least once from Arduino sketch to initialize the module.
110 \param freq Carrier frequency in MHz. Allowed values range from 860.0 MHz to 1020.0 MHz.
111 \param bw %LoRa link bandwidth in kHz. Allowed values are 125, 250 and 500 kHz.
112 \param sf %LoRa link spreading factor. Allowed values range from 6 to 12.
113 \param cr %LoRa link coding rate denominator. Allowed values range from 4 to 8. Note that a value of 4 means no coding,
114 is undocumented and not recommended without your own FEC.
115 \param syncWord %LoRa sync word. Can be used to distinguish different networks. Note that value 0x34 is reserved for LoRaWAN networks.
116 \param power Transmission output power in dBm. Allowed values range from 2 to 17 dBm.
117 \param preambleLength Length of %LoRa transmission preamble in symbols. The actual preamble length is 4.25 symbols longer than the set number.
118 Allowed values range from 6 to 65535.
119 \param gain Gain of receiver LNA (low-noise amplifier). Can be set to any integer in range 1 to 6 where 1 is the highest gain.
120 Set to 0 to enable automatic gain control (recommended).
121 \returns \ref status_codes
122 */
123 virtual int16_t begin(float freq = 915.0, float bw = 125.0, uint8_t sf = 9, uint8_t cr = 7, uint8_t syncWord = RADIOLIB_SX127X_SYNC_WORD, int8_t power = 10, uint16_t preambleLength = 8, uint8_t gain = 0);
124
125 /*!
126 \brief FSK modem initialization method. Must be called at least once from Arduino sketch to initialize the module.
127 \param freq Carrier frequency in MHz. Allowed values range from 860.0 MHz to 1020.0 MHz.
128 \param br Bit rate of the FSK transmission in kbps (kilobits per second). Allowed values range from 1.2 to 300.0 kbps.
129 \param freqDev Frequency deviation of the FSK transmission in kHz. Allowed values range from 0.6 to 200.0 kHz.
130 Note that the allowed range changes based on bit rate setting, so that the condition FreqDev + BitRate/2 <= 250 kHz is always met.
131 \param rxBw Receiver bandwidth in kHz. Allowed values are 2.6, 3.1, 3.9, 5.2, 6.3, 7.8, 10.4, 12.5, 15.6, 20.8, 25, 31.3, 41.7, 50, 62.5, 83.3, 100, 125, 166.7, 200 and 250 kHz.
132 \param power Transmission output power in dBm. Allowed values range from 2 to 17 dBm.
133 \param preambleLength Length of FSK preamble in bits.
134 \param enableOOK Use OOK modulation instead of FSK.
135 \returns \ref status_codes
136 */
137 int16_t beginFSK(float freq = 915.0, float br = 4.8, float freqDev = 5.0, float rxBw = 125.0, int8_t power = 10, uint16_t preambleLength = 16, bool enableOOK = false);
138
139 /*!
140 \brief Reset method. Will reset the chip to the default state using RST pin.
141 */
142 void reset() override;
143
144 // configuration methods
145
146 /*!
147 \brief Sets carrier frequency. Allowed values range from 860.0 MHz to 1020.0 MHz.
148 \param freq Carrier frequency to be set in MHz.
149 \returns \ref status_codes
150 */
151 int16_t setFrequency(float freq) override;
152
153 /*!
154 \brief Sets %LoRa link bandwidth. Allowed values are 125, 250 and 500 kHz. Only available in %LoRa mode.
155 \param bw %LoRa link bandwidth to be set in kHz.
156 \returns \ref status_codes
157 */
158 int16_t setBandwidth(float bw);
159
160 /*!
161 \brief Sets %LoRa link spreading factor. Allowed values range from 6 to 12. Only available in %LoRa mode.
162 \param sf %LoRa link spreading factor to be set.
163 \returns \ref status_codes
164 */
165 virtual int16_t setSpreadingFactor(uint8_t sf);
166
167 /*!
168 \brief Sets %LoRa link coding rate denominator. Allowed values range from 4 to 8. Only available in %LoRa mode.
169 Note that a value of 4 means no coding, is undocumented and not recommended without your own FEC.
170 \param cr %LoRa link coding rate denominator to be set.
171 \returns \ref status_codes
172 */
173 int16_t setCodingRate(uint8_t cr);
174
175 /*!
176 \brief Sets FSK bit rate. Allowed values range from 0.5 to 300 kbps. Only available in FSK mode.
177 \param br Bit rate to be set (in kbps).
178 \returns \ref status_codes
179 */
180 int16_t setBitRate(float br) override;
181
182 /*!
183 \brief Set data rate.
184 \param dr Data rate struct.
185 \param modem The modem corresponding to the requested datarate (FSK or LoRa).
186 Defaults to currently active modem if not supplied.
187 \returns \ref status_codes
188 */
189 int16_t setDataRate(DataRate_t dr, ModemType_t modem = RADIOLIB_MODEM_NONE) override;
190
191 /*!
192 \brief Check the data rate can be configured by this module.
193 \param dr Data rate struct.
194 \param modem The modem corresponding to the requested datarate (FSK or LoRa).
195 Defaults to currently active modem if not supplied.
196 \returns \ref status_codes
197 */
198 int16_t checkDataRate(DataRate_t dr, ModemType_t modem = RADIOLIB_MODEM_NONE) override;
199
200 /*!
201 \brief Sets transmission output power. Allowed values range from -1 to 14 dBm (RFO pin) or +2 to +20 dBm (PA_BOOST pin).
202 High power +20 dBm operation is also supported, on the PA_BOOST pin. Defaults to PA_BOOST.
203 \param power Transmission output power in dBm.
204 \returns \ref status_codes
205 */
206 int16_t setOutputPower(int8_t power) override;
207
208 /*!
209 \brief Sets transmission output power. Allowed values range from -1 to 14 dBm (RFO pin) or +2 to +20 dBm (PA_BOOST pin).
210 \param power Transmission output power in dBm.
211 \param forceRfo Whether to force using the RFO pin for the RF output (true)
212 or to leave the selection up to user (false) based on power output.
213 \returns \ref status_codes
214 */
215 int16_t setOutputPower(int8_t power, bool forceRfo);
216
217 /*!
218 \brief Check if output power is configurable.
219 This method is needed for compatibility with PhysicalLayer::checkOutputPower.
220 \param power Output power in dBm, assumes PA_BOOST pin.
221 \param clipped Clipped output power value to what is possible within the module's range.
222 \returns \ref status_codes
223 */
224 int16_t checkOutputPower(int8_t power, int8_t* clipped) override;
225
226 /*!
227 \brief Check if output power is configurable.
228 \param power Output power in dBm.
229 \param clipped Clipped output power value to what is possible within the module's range.
230 \param useRfo Whether to use the RFO (true) or the PA_BOOST (false) pin for the RF output.
231 \returns \ref status_codes
232 */
233 int16_t checkOutputPower(int8_t power, int8_t* clipped, bool useRfo);
234
235 /*!
236 \brief Sets gain of receiver LNA (low-noise amplifier). Can be set to any integer in range 1 to 6 where 1 is the highest gain.
237 Set to 0 to enable automatic gain control (recommended).
238 \param gain Gain of receiver LNA (low-noise amplifier) to be set.
239 \returns \ref status_codes
240 */
241 int16_t setGain(uint8_t gain);
242
243 /*!
244 \brief Sets Gaussian filter bandwidth-time product that will be used for data shaping. Only available in FSK mode with FSK modulation.
245 Allowed values are RADIOLIB_SHAPING_0_3, RADIOLIB_SHAPING_0_5 or RADIOLIB_SHAPING_1_0. Set to RADIOLIB_SHAPING_NONE to disable data shaping.
246 \param sh Gaussian shaping bandwidth-time product that will be used for data shaping
247 \returns \ref status_codes
248 */
249 int16_t setDataShaping(uint8_t sh) override;
250
251 /*!
252 \brief Sets filter cutoff frequency that will be used for data shaping.
253 Allowed values are 1 for frequency equal to bit rate and 2 for frequency equal to 2x bit rate. Set to 0 to disable data shaping.
254 Only available in FSK mode with OOK modulation.
255 \param sh Cutoff frequency that will be used for data shaping
256 \returns \ref status_codes
257 */
258 int16_t setDataShapingOOK(uint8_t sh);
259
260 /*!
261 \brief Gets received signal strength indicator.
262 Overload with packet mode enabled for PhysicalLayer compatibility.
263 \returns RSSI value in dBm.
264 */
265 float getRSSI() override;
266
267 /*!
268 \brief Gets received signal strength indicator.
269 \param packet Whether to read last packet RSSI, or the current value. LoRa mode only, ignored for FSK.
270 \param skipReceive Set to true to skip putting radio in receive mode for the RSSI measurement in FSK/OOK mode.
271 \returns RSSI value in dBm.
272 */
273 float getRSSI(bool packet, bool skipReceive = false);
274
275 /*!
276 \brief Enables/disables CRC check of received packets.
277 \param enable Enable (true) or disable (false) CRC.
278 \param mode Set CRC mode to RADIOLIB_SX127X_CRC_WHITENING_TYPE_CCITT for CCITT,
279 polynomial X16 + X12 + X5 + 1 (false) or RADIOLIB_SX127X_CRC_WHITENING_TYPE_IBM for IBM,
280 polynomial X16 + X15 + X2 + 1 (true). Only valid in FSK mode.
281 \returns \ref status_codes
282 */
283 int16_t setCRC(bool enable, bool mode = false);
284
285 /*!
286 \brief Forces LoRa low data rate optimization. Only available in LoRa mode. After calling this method, LDRO will always be set to
287 the provided value, regardless of symbol length. To re-enable automatic LDRO configuration, call SX1278::autoLDRO()
288 \param enable Force LDRO to be always enabled (true) or disabled (false).
289 \returns \ref status_codes
290 */
291 int16_t forceLDRO(bool enable);
292
293 /*!
294 \brief Re-enables automatic LDRO configuration. Only available in LoRa mode. After calling this method, LDRO will be enabled automatically
295 when symbol length exceeds 16 ms.
296 \returns \ref status_codes
297 */
298 int16_t autoLDRO();
299
300 /*!
301 \brief Set implicit header mode for future reception/transmission. Required for spreading factor 6.
302 \param len Payload length in bytes.
303 \returns \ref status_codes
304 */
305 int16_t implicitHeader(size_t len);
306
307 /*!
308 \brief Set explicit header mode for future reception/transmission.
309 \returns \ref status_codes
310 */
311 int16_t explicitHeader();
312
313 /*!
314 \brief Set modem for the radio to use. Will perform full reset and reconfigure the radio
315 using its default parameters.
316 \param modem Modem type to set - FSK or LoRa.
317 \returns \ref status_codes
318 */
319 int16_t setModem(ModemType_t modem) override;
320
321#if !RADIOLIB_GODMODE
322 protected:
323#endif
324 int16_t setBandwidthRaw(uint8_t newBandwidth);
325 int16_t setSpreadingFactorRaw(uint8_t newSpreadingFactor);
326 int16_t setCodingRateRaw(uint8_t newCodingRate);
327
328 int16_t configFSK() override;
329 void errataFix(bool rx) override;
330
331};
332
333#endif
